insert into FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp1_50 SELECT DISTINCT FIELDCOD FROM ZNMAT065  ;
insert into ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp1_50 SELECT DISTINCT ORGANLEAF FROM ZNMAT046 join FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp1_50 on ZNMAT046.ORGANCOD = FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp1_50.FIELDCOD  ;
insert into DATYPE_ZNMAT088temp1_50 SELECT DISTINCT DATYPE FROM ZNMAT088 ;
insert into FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp2_50 SELECT DISTINCT FIELDCOD FROM ZNMAT065  ;
insert into ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_50 SELECT DISTINCT ORGANLEAF FROM ZNMAT046 join FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp2_50 on ZNMAT046.ORGANCOD = FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp2_50.FIELDCOD  ;
insert into FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp3_50  SELECT DISTINCT FIELDCOD FROM ZNMAT065  ;
insert into LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp1_50 SELECT DISTINCT LINELEAF FROM ZNMAT024 join FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp3_50 on ZNMAT024.LINECOD = FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp3_50.FIELDCOD  ;
insert into LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp1_50  SELECT DISTINCT LOB_COKEY FROM ZNMAT021 join LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp1_50 on ZNMAT021.LOB_WD_VAL = LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp1_50.LINELEAF  ;
insert into ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_50  SELECT DISTINCT ORGANLEAF FROM ZNMAT046  ;
insert into LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp2_50 SELECT DISTINCT LINELEAF FROM ZNMAT024  ;
insert into LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_50  SELECT DISTINCT LOB_COKEY FROM ZNMAT021 join LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp2_50 on ZNMAT021.LOB_WD_VAL = LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp2_50.LINELEAF  ;
insert into LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp3_50 SELECT DISTINCT LINELEAF FROM ZNMAT024  ;
insert into LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp3_50  SELECT DISTINCT LOB_COKEY FROM ZNMAT021 join LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp3_50 on ZNMAT021.LOB_WD_VAL = LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp3_50.LINELEAF  ;
insert into he_temp_50(SEQNR,HE)SELECT SEQNR, MAX(opexpenses)  AS HE FROM ZNMAT011 AS ZTAB  join ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp1_50 on ZTAB.OPTNAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp1_50.ORGANLEAF   join DATYPE_ZNMAT088temp1_50 on ZTAB.DATYPE=DATYPE_ZNMAT088temp1_50.DATYPE   GROUP BY SEQNR;
insert into he_temp2_50(SEQNR,HE)SELECT SEQNR, MAX(opexpenses)  AS HE FROM ZNMAT011 AS ZTAB  join ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp1_50 on ZTAB.OPTNAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp1_50.ORGANLEAF   join DATYPE_ZNMAT088temp1_50 on ZTAB.DATYPE=DATYPE_ZNMAT088temp1_50.DATYPE   GROUP BY SEQNR;
insert into he_temp3_50(SEQNR,HE)SELECT SEQNR, MAX(opexpenses)  AS HE FROM ZNMAT011 AS ZTAB  join ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp1_50 on ZTAB.OPTNAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp1_50.ORGANLEAF   join DATYPE_ZNMAT088temp1_50 on ZTAB.DATYPE=DATYPE_ZNMAT088temp1_50.DATYPE   GROUP BY SEQNR;
insert into PRDLEAF_ZNMAT023temp1_50(PRDLEAF) SELECT DISTINCT PRDLEAF FROM ZNMAT023  ;
insert into PRD_COKEY_ZNMAT020temp1_50(PRD_COKEY)SELECT DISTINCT PRD_COKEY FROM ZNMAT020 join PRDLEAF_ZNMAT023temp1_50 on PRDLEAF_ZNMAT023temp1_50.PRDLEAF=ZNMAT020.PRD_WD_VAL   ;
